| Goal | Tool |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Task: Rename _engine to _index_engine in Index

## Objective
Rename the `_engine` property/attribute to `_index_engine` in `pandas/core/indexes/base.py`
and all subclasses to avoid naming collisions and improve clarity.

## Requirements

1. **Rename in base class** `pandas/core/indexes/base.py`:
   - `_engine` property → `_index_engine`
   - Update cache decorators and lazy evaluation

2. **Update all subclass overrides** (20+ references):
   - `pandas/core/indexes/range.py`
   - `pandas/core/indexes/multi.py`
   - `pandas/core/indexes/datetimes.py`
   - `pandas/core/indexes/period.py`
   - Internal callers

3. **Update internal callers** that access `._engine`

## Key Reference Files
- `pandas/core/indexes/base.py` — base Index with _engine
- `pandas/core/indexes/range.py` — RangeIndex override
- `pandas/core/indexes/multi.py` — MultiIndex
- `pandas/_libs/index.pyx` — Cython engine implementations

## Success Criteria
- `_engine` no longer used as property name in Index
- `_index_engine` used instead
- Subclass overrides updated
- Internal callers updated (80%+)

Running command: cat << 'PYEOF' > /tmp/process_content.py
import re
import sys
import json

def strip_line_numbers(content):
    """Remove the 'NN: ' prefix from each line in the read_file output."""
    lines = content.split('\n')
    result = []
    for line in lines:
        # Match "NNN: " at start (line numbers can be 1-5 digits)
        m = re.match(r'^\d+: (.*)', line)
        if m:
            result.append(m.group(1))
        else:
            result.append(line)
    return '\n'.join(result)

if __name__ == '__main__':
    # Test the function
    test = "1: hello\n2: world\n10: foo\n100: bar"
    print(strip_line_numbers(test))
PYEOF

import re
import os
import shutil

def apply_rename(src_path, dest_path):
    """Apply _engine -> _index_engine rename to a file."""
    with open(src_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
        content = f.read()
    
    original = content
    
    # 1. Rename property/method definitions: def _engine( -> def _index_engine(
    content = re.sub(r'\bdef _engine\(', 'def _index_engine(', content)
    
    # 2. Rename all property accesses: ._engine -> ._index_engine
    #    Use word boundary to avoid hitting _engine_type, _engine_types
    content = re.sub(r'\._engine\b', '._index_engine', content)
    
    # 3. Rename the cache key string: "_engine" -> "_index_engine"
    #    This is for cache_readonly which stores results with function name as key
    content = content.replace('"_engine"', '"_index_engine"')
    
    # Verify some changes were made
    os.makedirs(os.path.dirname(dest_path), exist_ok=True)
    with open(dest_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
        f.write(content)
    
    # Count changes
    changes = sum(1 for a, b in zip(original.splitlines(), content.splitlines()) if a != b)
    return changes

# Source files (downloaded from GitHub)
# Destination files (workspace)
file_pairs = [
    ('/tmp/pandas/core/indexes/base.py', '/workspace/pandas/core/indexes/base.py'),

    ('/tmp/pandas/core/indexes/interval.py', '/workspace/pandas/core/indexes/interval.py'),
    ('/tmp/pandas/core/indexes/category.py', '/workspace/pandas/core/indexes/category.py'),

import re, os

def apply_rename(src, dest):
    with open(src, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
        content = f.read()
    original = content
    content = re.sub(r'\bdef _engine\(', 'def _index_engine(', content)

    os.makedirs(os.path.dirname(dest), exist_ok=True)
